{\n            if (range.start <= range.end) {\n                // Normal period (e.g., morning: 6-10)\n                if (hour >= range.start && hour < range.end) {\n                    period =                period = key;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Remove all time periods\n        document.body.classList.remove('time-morning', ============================================\n\n    /**\n     * Connect to WebSocket for real-time updates\n     */\n    function connectWebSocket() {\n        // Disconnect existing connection\n data.blobs;\n            if (data.portals) currentState.portals = data.portals;\n            if (data.nodes) currentState.nodes = data.nodes;\n            if (data.events) currentState.alerts = currentState.nodesTotal = currentState.nodes.length;\n\n            currentState.lastUpdate = new Date();\n\n            // Update renderer state\n            if (renderer) {\n                renderer.updateState(currentState);\n            }\n\n            // Update UI\n            updateStatus();\n            checkAlerts();\n\n            // Trigger first detection for briefing\n            if (currentState.blobs.length > 0 && window.SpaxelAmbientBriefing) {\n                window.SpaxelAmbientBriefing.onFirstDetection();\n            }\n\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Handle loc_update messages (event-driven blob updates)\n        if (data.type === 'loc_update') {\n            if (data.blobs) {\n                currentState.blobs = data.blobs;\n            }\n            currentState.lastUpdate = new Date();\n\n            // Update renderer state\n            if (renderer) {\n                renderer.updateState(currentState);\n            }\n\n            // Update UI\n            updateStatus();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Handle event-driven messages\n        if (data.type === 'alert' || data.type === 'anomaly_detected' || data.type === 'fall_alert') {\n            // Add to alerts\n            const exists = currentState.alerts.some(a => a.id === data.id);\n            if (!exists) {\n                currentState.alerts.push(data);\n            }\n            currentState.lastUpdate = new Date();\n            checkAlerts();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Handle system_mode_change for security mode\n        if (data.type === 'system_mode_change') {\n            if (data.security_mode !== undefined) {\n                currentState.securityMode = data.security_mode;\n            }\n            updateStatus();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Handle delta messages (no type field - incremental updates)\n        if (!data.type) {\n            if (data.blobs) {\n                currentState.blobs = data.blobs;\n            }\n            if (data.zones) {\n                currentState.zones = data.zones;\n            }\n            if (data.portals) {\n                currentState.portals = data.portals;\n            }\n            if (data.nodes) {\n                currentState.nodes = data.nodes;\n                currentState.nodesOnline = currentState.nodes.filter(n => n.status === 'online').length;\n                currentState.nodesTotal = currentState.nodes.length;\n            }\n            if (data.events && data.events.length > 0) {\n                // Add new alerts\n                data.events.forEach(event => {\n                    if (event.type === 'alert' || event.type === 'fall_alert' || event.type === 'anomaly') {\n                        // Check if alert already exists\n                        const exists = currentState.alerts.some(a => a.id === event.id);\n                        if (!exists) {\n                            currentState.alerts.push(event);\n                        }\n                    }\n                });\n            }\n            // Handle security_mode in delta\n            if (data.security_mode !== undefined) {\n                currentState.securityMode = data.security_mode;\n            }\n\n            currentState.lastUpdate = new Date();\n\n            // Update renderer state\n            if (renderer) {\n                renderer.updateState(currentState);\n            }\n\n            // Update UI\n            updateStatus();\n            checkAlerts();\n        }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Status Updates\n    // ============================================\n\n    /**\n     * Update status bar\n     */\n    function updateStatus() {\n        const statusText = document.getElementById('ambient-status-text');\n        const timeDisplay = document.getElementById('ambient-time');\n        const nodesDisplay = document.getElementById('ambient-nodes');\n        const secureMessage = document.getElementById('ambient-secure');\n\n        if (statusText) {\n            // Determine status based on alerts and security mode\n            if (currentState.alerts.length > 0) {\n                statusText.textContent = 'Alert active';\n            } else if (currentState.securityMode) {\n                statusText.textContent = 'Security armed';\n            } else {\n                statusText.textContent = 'All secure';\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (timeDisplay) {\n            const now });\n        }\n\n        if (nodesDisplay) {\n            nodesDisplay.textContent = `${currentState.nodesOnline}/${currentState.nodesTotal} nodes`;\n        }\n\n        // Show/hide \"All Secure\" message\n        if (secureMessage) {\n            const hasPeople = currentState.blobs.length > 0;\n            const hasAlerts = currentState.alerts.length > 0;\n\n            if (!hasPeople && !hasAlerts && !isDimmed()) {\n                secureMessage.style.display = 'block';\n            } else {\n                secureMessage.style.display = 'none';\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    function isDimmed() {\n        return renderer && document.getElementById('ambient-canvas')?.style.filter.includes('brightness(0.4)');\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Check for alerts and show/hide alert mode\n     */\n    function checkAlerts() {\n        if (currentState.alerts.length > 0) {\n            // Show alert mode in renderer\n            if (renderer) {\n                const latestAlert = currentState.alerts[0];\n                renderer.enterAlertMode(latestAlert);\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Hide alert mode\n            if (renderer) {\n                renderer.exitAlertMode();\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Handle alert click/acknowledge\n     */\n    function handleAlertClick(alert) {\n        // Dismiss the alert\n showToast('Alert acknowledged', 'info');\n\n        // Check for fall alerts - POST to acknowledge endpoint\n        if (alert.type === 'fall_alert' && alert.id) {\n            acknowledgeAlert(alert.id, 'fall');\n        } else if (alert.type === 'anomaly' && alert.id) {\n            acknowledgeAlert(alert.id, 'anomaly');\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Acknowledge an Remove blobs that are no longer tracked\n156\t                const trackedIds = new Set(state.blobs.map(b => b.id));\n157\t                for (const id of currentPositions.keys()) {\n158\t                    if (!trackedIds.has(id)) {\n159\t                        currentPositions.delete(id);\n160\t                        targetPositions.delete(id);\n161\t                    }\n162\t                }\n163\t            }\n164\t\n165\t            // Update state\n166\t            if (state.zones) currentState.zones = state.zones;\n167\t            if (state.portals) currentState.portals = state.portals;\n168\t            if (state.nodes) currentState.nodes = state.nodes;\n169\t            if (state.alerts) currentState.alerts = state.alerts;\n170\t            if (state.security_mode !== undefined) currentState.securityMode = state.security_mode;\n171\t            currentState.lastUpdate = new Date();\n172\t\n173\t            // Check for alerts to update system health\n174\t            updateSystemHealth();\n175\t\n176\t            // Check for presence in ambient zone (for auto-dim)\n177\t            checkAmbientZonePresence();\n178\t        },\n179\t\n180\t        /**\n181\t         * Set the ambient zone for auto-dim detection\n182\t         * @param {string} zoneId - Zone ID to monitor for presence\n183\t         */\n184\t        setAmbientZone(zoneId) {\n185\t            config.ambientZone = zoneId;\n186\t            console.log('[AmbientRenderer] Ambient zone set to:', zoneId);\n187\t        },\n188\t\n189\t        /**\n190\t         * Set alert click callback\n191\t         * @param {Function} callback - Function to call when alert is clicked\n192\t         */\n193\t        setAlertClickCallback(callback) {\n194\t            onAlertClick = callback;\n195\t        },\n196\t\n197\t        /**\n198\t         * Set user activity callback\n199\t         * @param {Function} callback - Function to call on user activity\n200\t         */\n201\t        setUserActivityCallback(callback) {\n202\t            onUserActivity = callback;\n203\t        },\n204\t\n205\t        /**\n206\t         * Manually trigger a render\n207\t         */\n208\t        render() {\n209\t            if (ctx && canvas) {\n210\t                renderFrame();\n211\t            }\n212\t        },\n213\t\n214\t        /**\n215\t         * Enter alert mode\n216\t         * @param {Object} alert - Alert data\n217\t         */\n218\t        enterAlertMode(alert) {\n219\t            currentState.alerts = [alert];\n220\t            startAlertPulse();\n221\t        },\n222\t\n223\t        /**\n224\t         * Exit alert mode\n225\t         */\n226\t        exitAlertMode() {\n227\t            currentState.alerts = [];\n228\t            stopAlertPulse();\n229\t        },\n230\t\n231\t        /**\n232\t         * Wake from dim mode\n233\t         */\n234\t        wakeFromDim() {\n235\t            if (isDimmed) {\n236\t                isDimmed = false;\n237\t                canvas.style.filter = 'brightness(1)';\n238\t                canvas.style.transition = 'filter 0.3s ease';\n239\t                resetDimTimer();\n240\t            }\n241\t        },\n242\t\n243\t        /**\n244\t         * Get current time period\n245\t         * @returns {string} - 'morning', 'day', 'evening', or 'night'\n246\t         */\n247\t        getTimePeriod() {\n248\t            const hour = new Date().getHours();\n249\t            if (hour >= 6 && hour < 10) return 'morning';\n250\t            if (hour >= 10 && hour < 18) return 'day';\n251\t            if (hour >= 18 && hour < 22) return 'evening';\n252\t            return 'night';\n253\t        },\n254\t\n255\t        /**\n256\t         * Clean up resources\n257\t         */\n258\t        destroy() {\n259\t            stopRenderLoop();\n260\t            stopAlertPulse();\n261\t            if (dimTimer) {\n262\t                clearTimeout(dimTimer);\n263\t                dimTimer = null;\n264\t            }\n265\t            window.removeEventListener('resize', resizeCanvas);\n266\t            console.log('[AmbientRenderer] Destroyed');\n267\t        },\n268\t\n269\t        /**\n270\t         * Stop the render loop (for testing)\n271\t         */\n272\t        stopRenderLoop() {\n273\t            stopRenderLoop();\n274\t        },\n275\t\n276\t        /**\n277\t         * Start the render loop (for testing)\n278\t         */\n279\t        startRenderLoop() {\n280\t            startRenderLoop();\n281\t        },\n282\t\n283\t        // Testing/internal methods\n284\t        _getCurrentState,\n285\t        _getCurrentPositions,\n286\t        _getTargetPositions,\n287\t        _getAlertPulseState,\n288\t        _getRenderCallCount,\n289\t        _resetRenderCallCount,\n290\t        _enterDimMode,\n291\t        _checkAmbientZonePresence\n292\t    };\n293\t\n294\t    // ============================================\n295\t    // Internal Functions\n296\t    // ============================================\n297\t\n298\t    function resizeCanvas() {\n299\t        if (!canvas) return;\n300\t\n301\t        const container = canvas.parentElement;\n302\t        if (!container) return;\n303\t\n304\t        const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();\n305\t        const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;\n306\t\n307\t        canvas.width = rect.width * dpr;\n308\t        canvas.height = rect.height * dpr;\n309\t        canvas.style.width = rect.width + 'px';\n310\t        canvas.style.height = rect.height + 'px';\n311\t\n312\t        if (ctx) {\n313\t            ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);\n314\t        }\n315\t    }\n316\t\n317\t    function startRenderLoop() {\n318\t        stopRenderLoop();\n319\t\n320\t        function renderLoop(timestamp) {\n321\t            // Throttle to 2 Hz (500ms between frames)\n322\t            if (timestamp - lastRenderTime >= RENDER_INTERVAL_MS) {\n323\t                lastRenderTime = timestamp;\n324\t                renderFrame();\n325\t            }\n326\t            renderTimer = requestAnimationFrame(renderLoop);\n327\t        }\n328\t\n329\t        renderTimer = requestAnimationFrame(renderLoop);\n330\t    }\n331\t\n332\t    function stopRenderLoop() {\n333\t        if (renderTimer) {\n334\t            cancelAnimationFrame(renderTimer);\n335\t            renderTimer = null;\n336\t        }\n337\t    }\n338\t\n339\t    function renderFrame() {\n340\t        if (!ctx || !canvas) return;\n341\t\n342\t        renderCallCount++; // Track render calls for testing\n343\t\n344\t        const width = canvas.width / (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);\n345\t        const height = canvas.height / (window.devicePixelRatio || 1);\n346\t\n347\t        // Clear canvas\n348\t        ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);\n349\t\n350\t        // Get current time period and colors\n351\t        const period = AmbientRenderer.getTimePeriod();\n352\t        const colors = TIME_COLORS[period];\n353\t\n354\t        // Draw background\n355\t        drawBackground(ctx, width, height, colors);\n356\t\n357\t        // Check for alert mode\n358\t        const hasActiveAlert = currentState.alerts.length > 0;\n359\t        if (hasActiveAlert) {\n360\t            drawAlertMode(ctx, width, height);\n361\t            return; // Alert mode takes over the entire canvas\n362\t        }\n363\t\n364\t        // Calculate floor plan bounds\n365\t        const bounds = calculateBounds(width, height);\n366\t\n367\t        // Draw zones (room outlines)\n368\t        drawZones(ctx, bounds, colors);\n369\t\n370\t        // Draw portals\n371\t        drawPortals(ctx, bounds, colors);\n372\t\n373\t        // Draw nodes\n374\t        drawNodes(ctx, bounds, colors);\n375\t\n376\t        // Draw people (with lerp-interpolated positions)\n377\t        drawPeople(ctx, bounds, colors);\n378\t\n379\t        // Draw system status indicator (top-left)\n380\t        drawSystemStatus(ctx, colors);\n381\t\n382\t        // Draw time display (top-right)\n383\t        drawTimeDisplay(ctx, width, colors);\n384\t    }\n385\t\n386\t    function drawBackground(ctx, width, height, colors) {\n387\t        // Solid background color based on time of day\n388\t        ctx.fillStyle = colors.bg;\n389\t        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);\n390\t    }\n391\t\n392\t    function drawAlertMode(ctx, width, height) {\n393\t        // Pulsing red background for alert mode\n394\t        const pulseIntensity = alertPulseState ? 1.0 : 0.7;\n395\t\n396\t        // Create gradient background\n397\t        const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(\n398\t            width / 2, height / 2, 0,\n399\t            width / 2, height / 2, Math.max(width, height) / 2\n400\t        );\n401\t        gradient.addColorStop(0, `rgba(220, 38, 38, ${pulseIntensity})`);\n402\t        gradient.addColorStop(1, `rgba(127, 29, 29, ${pulseIntensity * 0.8})`);\n403\t\n404\t        ctx.fillStyle = gradient;\n405\t        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);\n406\t\n407\t        // Draw pulsing border\n408\t        const borderWidth = 8 + (pulseIntensity * 4); // 8-12px\n409\t        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${pulseIntensity})`;\n410\t        ctx.lineWidth = borderWidth;\n411\t        ctx.strokeRect(0, 0, width, height);\n412\t\n413\t        // Draw alert text\n414\t        const alert = currentState.alerts[0];\n415\t        if (alert) {\n416\t            ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';\n417\t            ctx.font = 'bold 48px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';\n418\t            ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n419\t            ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';\n420\t\n421\t            const title = alert.type === 'fall_alert' ? 'FALL DETECTED' :\n422\t                          alert.type === 'anomaly' ? 'ANOMALY' : 'ALERT';\n423\t            const message = formatAlertMessage(alert);\n424\t\n425\t            ctx.fillText(title, width / 2, height / 2 - 30);\n426\t            ctx.font = '24px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';\n427\t            ctx.fillText(message, width / 2, height / 2 + 30);\n428\t\n429\t            // Draw acknowledge button\n430\t            const buttonWidth = 200;\n431\t            const buttonHeight = 60;\n432\t            const buttonX = (width - buttonWidth) / 2;\n433\t            const buttonY = height / 2 + 80;\n434\t\n435\t            // Button background with glow\n436\t            ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${0.9 + pulseIntensity * 0.1})`;\n437\t            ctx.shadowColor = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.5)';\n438\t            ctx.shadowBlur = 10;\n439\t            ctx.beginPath();\n440\t            ctx.roundRect(buttonX, buttonY, buttonWidth, buttonHeight, 8);\n441\t            ctx.fill();\n442\t            ctx.shadowBlur = 0;\n443\t\n444\t            ctx.fillStyle = '#dc2626';\n445\t            ctx.font = 'bold 20px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';\n446\t            ctx.fillText('Acknowledge', width / 2, buttonY + buttonHeight / 2);\n447\t        }\n448\t    }\n449\t\n450\t    function formatAlertMessage(alert) {\n451\t        if (alert.type === 'fall_alert') {\n452\t            const person = alert.person || 'Someone';\n453\t            return `${person} has fallen`;\n454\t        } else if (alert.type === 'anomaly') {\n455\t            return 'Unusual activity detected';\n456\t        }\n457\t        return 'Alert detected';\n458\t    }\n459\t\n460\t    function calculateBounds(canvasWidth, canvasHeight) {\n461\t        // Find bounds of all zones\n462\t        if (currentState.zones.length === 0) {\n463\t            // Default bounds - centered square\n464\t            const size = Math.min(canvasWidth, canvasHeight) - config.margin * 2;\n465\t            return {\n466\t                x: (canvasWidth - size) / 2,\n467\t                y: (canvasHeight - size) / 2,\n468\t                width: size,\n469\t                height: size,\n470\t                scale: size / 10, // 10 meters default\n471\t                minX: 0,\n472\t                minY: 0\n473\t            };\n474\t        }\n475\t\n476\t        let minX = Infinity, minY = Infinity;\n477\t        let maxX = -Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;\n478\t\n479\t        currentState.zones.forEach(zone => {\n480\t            const x = zone.x || zone.MinX || 0;\n481\t            const y = zone.y || zone.MinY || 0;\n482\t            const w = zone.w || zone.SizeX || zone.w || 1;\n483\t            const d = zone.d || zone.SizeY || zone.d || 1;\n484\t\n485\t            minX = Math.min(minX, x);\n486\t            minY = Math.min(minY, y);\n487\t            maxX = Math.max(maxX, x + w);\n488\t            maxY = Math.max(maxY, y + d);\n489\t        });\n490\t\n491\t        // Add margin\n492\t        const marginMeters = 1; // 1 meter margin\n493\t        minX -= marginMeters;\n494\t        minY -= marginMeters;\n495\t        maxX += marginMeters;\n496\t        maxY += marginMeters;\n497\t\n498\t        const floorWidth = maxX - minX;\n499\t        const floorHeight = maxY - minY;\n500\t\n501\t        // Calculate scale to fit canvas\n502\t        const scaleX = (canvasWidth - config.margin * 2) / floorWidth;\n503\t        const scaleY = (canvasHeight - config.margin * 2) / floorHeight;\n504\t        const scale = Math.min(scaleX, scaleY, config.scale);\n505\t\n506\t        // Calculate centered bounds\n507\t        const boundsWidth = floorWidth * scale;\n508\t        const boundsHeight = floorHeight * scale;\n509\t        const boundsX = (canvasWidth - boundsWidth) / 2;\n510\t        const boundsY = (canvasHeight - boundsHeight) / 2;\n511\t\n512\t        return {\n513\t            x: boundsX,\n514\t            y: boundsY,\n515\t            width: boundsWidth,\n516\t            height: boundsHeight,\n517\t            scale: scale,\n518\t            minX: minX,\n519\t            minY: minY\n520\t        };\n521\t    }\n522\t\n523\t    function worldToScreen(wx, wy, bounds) {\n524\t        return {\n525\t            x: bounds.x + (wx - bounds.minX) * bounds.scale,\n526\t            y: bounds.y + (wy - bounds.minY) * bounds.scale\n527\t        };\n528\t    }\n529\t\n530\t    function drawZones(ctx, bounds, colors) {\n531\t        currentState.zones.forEach(zone => {\n532\t            const x = zone.x || zone.MinX || 0;\n533\t            const y = zone.y || zone.MinY || 0;\n534\t            const w = zone.w || zone.SizeX || 1;\n535\t            const d = zone.d || zone.SizeY || 1;\n536\t\n537\t            const topLeft = worldToScreen(x, y, bounds);\n538\t            const width = w * bounds.scale;\n539\t            const height = d * bounds.scale;\n540\t\n541\t            // Zone outline (white, 1px stroke)\n542\t            ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffffff';\n543\t            ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n544\t            ctx.strokeRect(topLeft.x, topLeft.y, width, height);\n545\t\n546\t            // Zone label at centroid\n547\t            const centerX = topLeft.x + width / 2;\n548\t            const centerY = topLeft.y + height / 2;\n549\t\n550\t            const count = zone.count || zone.occupancy || 0;\n551\t            const zoneName = zone.name || zone.Name || 'Zone';\n552\t\n553\t            ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';\n554\t            ctx.font = '14px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';\n555\t            ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n556\t            ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';\n557\t            ctx.fillText(zoneName, centerX, centerY);\n558\t\n559\t            if (count > 0) {\n560\t                ctx.font = '12px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';\n561\t                ctx.fillText(`(${count})`, centerX, centerY + 16);\n562\t            }\n563\t        });\n564\t    }\n565\t\n566\t    function drawPortals(ctx, bounds, colors) {\n567\t        if (!currentState.portals || currentState.portals.length === 0) {\n568\t            return;\n569\t        }\n570\t\n571\t        ctx.strokeStyle = '#a855f7'; // Purple\n572\t        ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;\n573\t\n574\t        currentState.portals.forEach(portal => {\n575\t            // Portal is defined by two points\n576\t            const p1 = worldToScreen(portal.p1_x || 0, portal.p1_y || 0, bounds);\n577\t            const p2 = worldToScreen(portal.p2_x || 0, portal.p2_y || 0, bounds);\n578\t\n579\t            ctx.beginPath();\n580\t            ctx.moveTo(p1.x, p1.y);\n581\t            ctx.lineTo(p2.x, p2.y);\n582\t            ctx.stroke();\n583\t        });\n584\t    }\n585\t\n586\t    function drawNodes(ctx, bounds, colors) {\n587\t        currentState.nodes.forEach(node => {\n588\t            const x = node.pos_x || node.PosX || 0;\n589\t            const y = node.pos_y || node.PosY || 0;\n590\t\n591\t            const pos = worldToScreen(x, y, bounds);\n592\t\n593\t            // Small filled circle (4px radius)\n594\t            ctx.fillStyle = '#6b7280'; // Grey\n595\t            ctx.beginPath();\n596\t            ctx.arc(pos.x, pos.y, 4, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n597\t            ctx.fill();\n598\t        });\n599\t    }\n600\t\n601\t    function drawPeople(ctx, bounds, colors) {\n602\t        currentState.blobs.forEach(blob => {\n603\t            // Get current position (with lerp interpolation)\n604\t            let pos = currentPositions.get(blob.id);\n605\t            if (!pos) {\n606\t                pos = { x: blob.x, y: blob.y, z: blob.z || 0 };\n607\t                currentPositions.set(blob.id, pos);\n608\t            }\n609\t\n610\t            // Get target position\n611\t            const target = targetPositions.get(blob.id);\n612\t            if (target) {\n613\t                // Lerp toward target (20% of remaining distance)\n614\t                pos.x = lerp(pos.x, target.x, LERP_FACTOR);\n615\t                pos.y = lerp(pos.y, target.y, LERP_FACTOR);\n616\t                pos.z = lerp(pos.z, target.z, LERP_FACTOR);\n617\t\n618\t                // Update the currentPositions map with the lerped position\n619\t                currentPositions.set(blob.id, { ...pos });\n620\t            }\n621\t\n622\t            const screenPos = worldToScreen(pos.x, pos.y, bounds);\n623\t\n624\t            // Blob radius proportional to identity confidence\n625\t            const confidence = blob.confidence || 0.5;\n626\t            const radius = 10 + (confidence * 8); // 10-18px\n627\t\n628\t            // Get person color\n629\t            let blobColor = '#6b7280'; // Grey for unknown\n630\t            // Handle both person_label (from backend) and person (for consistency)\n631\t            const personName = blob.person_label || blob.person || null;\n632\t            if (personName) {\n633\t                blobColor = getPersonColor(personName);\n634\t            }\n635\t\n636\t            // Draw person blob\n637\t            ctx.fillStyle = blobColor;\n638\t            ctx.beginPath();\n639\t            ctx.arc(screenPos.x, screenPos.y, radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n640\t            ctx.fill();\n641\t\n642\t            // Draw name label above\n643\t            const name = personName ? getFirstName(personName) : '?';\n644\t            ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';\n645\t            ctx.font = '12px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';\n646\t            ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n647\t            ctx.fillText(name, screenPos.x, screenPos.y - radius - 4);\n648\t        });\n649\t    }\n650\t\n651\t    function drawSystemStatus(ctx, colors) {\n652\t        const size = 16; // 8px radius = 16px diameter\n653\t        const margin = 16;\n654\t        const x = margin + size / 2;\n655\t        const y = margin + size / 2;\n656\t\n657\t        // Determine status color\n658\t        let statusColor;\n659\t        if (currentState.alerts.length > 0) {\n660\t            statusColor = '#ef4444'; // Red - alert\n661\t        } else {\n662\t            // Check node health\n663\t            const onlineNodes = currentState.nodes.filter(n => n.status === 'online').length;\n664\t            const totalNodes = currentState.nodes.length;\n665\t\n666\t            if (onlineNodes === 0 && totalNodes > 0) {\n667\t                statusColor = '#ef4444'; // Red - all offline\n668\t            } else if (onlineNodes < totalNodes) {\n669\t                statusColor = '#f59e0b'; // Amber - some degraded\n670\t            } else {\n671\t                statusColor = '#22c55e'; // Green - all healthy\n672\t            }\n673\t        }\n674\t\n675\t        // Draw status dot\n676\t        ctx.fillStyle = statusColor;\n677\t        ctx.beginPath();\n678\t        ctx.arc(x, y, 8, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n679\t        ctx.fill();\n680\t    }\n681\t\n682\t    function drawTimeDisplay(ctx, canvasWidth, colors) {\n683\t        const now = new Date();\n684\t        const timeStr = now.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {\n685\t            hour: 'numeric',\n686\t            minute: '2-digit',\n687\t            hour12: true\n688\t        });\n689\t\n690\t        ctx.fillStyle = colors.text;\n691\t        ctx.font = '28px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, monospace';\n692\t        ctx.textAlign = 'right';\n693\t        ctx.textBaseline = 'top';\n694\t        ctx.fillText(timeStr, canvasWidth - 16, 16);\n695\t    }\n696\t\n697\t    // ============================================\n698\t    // Auto-Dim Logic\n699\t    // ============================================\n700\t\n701\t    function resetDimTimer() {\n702\t        if (dimTimer) {\n703\t            clearTimeout(dimTimer);\n704\t        }\n705\t\n706\t        dimTimer = setTimeout(() => {\n707\t            enterDimMode();\n708\t        }, AUTO_DIM_TIMEOUT_MS);\n709\t    }\n710\t\n711\t    function enterDimMode() {\n712\t        isDimmed = true;\n713\t        // Reduce canvas brightness to 40%\n714\t        canvas.style.filter = 'brightness(0.4)';\n715\t        canvas.style.transition = 'filter 0.5s ease';\n716\t        console.log('[AmbientRenderer] Entered dim mode');\n717\t    }\n718\t\n719\t    function checkAmbientZonePresence() {\n720\t        if (!config.ambientZone) {\n721\t            return; // No ambient zone configured\n722\t        }\n723\t\n724\t        // Check if anyone is in the ambient zone\n725\t        const zone = currentState.zones.find(z => z.id === config.ambientZone || z.name === config.ambientZone);\n726\t        if (zone && (zone.count > 0 || zone.occupancy > 0)) {\n727\t            // Someone is present - wake from dim\n728\t            if (isDimmed) {\n729\t                AmbientRenderer.wakeFromDim();\n730\t            }\n731\t            // Reset the timer\n732\t            resetDimTimer();\n733\t        }\n734\t    }\n735\t\n736\t    // ============================================\n737\t    // Alert Pulse Animation\n738\t    // ============================================\n739\t\n740\t    function startAlertPulse() {\n741\t        if (alertPulseTimer) {\n742\t            return; // Already running\n743\t        }\n744\t\n745\t        alertPulseTimer = setInterval(() => {\n746\t            alertPulseState = !alertPulseState;\n747\t            // Force immediate render\n748\t            renderFrame();\n749\t        }, ALERT_PULSE_INTERVAL_MS);\n750\t    }\n751\t\n752\t    function stopAlertPulse() {\n753\t        if (alertPulseTimer) {\n754\t            clearInterval(alertPulseTimer);\n755\t            alertPulseTimer = null;\n756\t        }\n757\t        alertPulseState = false;\n758\t    }\n759\t\n760\t    // ============================================\n761\t    // Helper Functions\n762\t    // ============================================\n763\t\n764\t    function lerp(start, end, factor) {\n765\t        return start + (end - start) * factor;\n766\t    }\n767\t\n768\t    function getPersonColor(personName) {\n769\t        // Generate consistent color from name\n770\t        let hash = 0;\n771\t        for (let i = 0; i < personName.length; i++) {\n772\t            hash = personName.charCodeAt(i) + ((hash << 5) - hash);\n773\t        }\n774\t        const hue = Math.abs(hash) % 360;\n775\t        return `hsl(${hue}, 70%, 50%)`;\n776\t    }\n777\t\n778\t    function getFirstName(fullName) {\n779\t        if (!fullName) return '?';\n780\t        const parts = fullName.trim().split(/\\s+/);\n781\t        return parts[0];\n782\t    }\n783\t\n784\t    function updateSystemHealth() {\n785\t        if (currentState.alerts.length > 0) {\n786\t     init(canvasElement, rendererConfig = {}) {\n            canvas = canvasElement;\n            ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');\n\n            // Apply configuration\n            Object.assign(config,   }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Update state\n            if (state.zones) currentState.zones = state.zones;\n            if (state.portals) currentState.portals = getTimePeriod() {\n            const hour = new Date().getHours();\n            if (hour >= 6 && hour < 10) return 'morning';\n            if (hour >= 10 && hour < 18) return 'day';\n            if   const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();\n        const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;\n\n        canvas.width = rect.width * dpr;\n        canvas.height = rect.height * dpr;\n {\n        stopRenderLoop();\n\n        function renderLoop(timestamp) {\n            // Throttle to 2 Hz (500ms between frames)\n            if (timestamp - lastRenderTime >= RENDER_INTERVAL_MS) {\n                lastRenderTime = timestamp;\n                renderFrame();\n            }\n            renderTimer = requestAnimationFrame(renderLoop);\n        }\n\n        renderTimer =  }\n\n    function renderFrame() {\n        if (!ctx || !canvas) return;\n\n        renderCallCount++; // Track render calls for testing\n\n        const width = canvas.width / 8-12px\n        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${pulseIntensity})`;\n        ctx.lineWidth = borderWidth;\n        ctx.strokeRect(0, 0, width, height);\n\n        // Draw alert text\n ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n            ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';\n\n            const title = alert.type === 'fall_alert' ? 'FALL DETECTED' :\n                          alert.type === 'anomaly' ? BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';\n            ctx.fillText(message, width / 2, height / 2 + 30);\n\n            // Draw acknowledge button\n            const buttonWidth = 200;\n            const buttonHeight = 60;\n            const buttonX = (width - buttonWidth) / 2;\n            const buttonY = height / 2 + 80;\n\n            // Button background with glow\n            ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${0.9 + pulseIntensity * 0.1})`;\n            ctx.shadowColor = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.5)';\n            ctx.shadowBlur = 10;\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.roundRect(buttonX, buttonY, buttonWidth, buttonHeight, 8);\n            ctx.fill();\n            ctx.shadowBlur = 0;\n\n            ctx.fillStyle = '#dc2626';\n            ctx.font = 'bold 20px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';\n            ctx.fillText('Acknowledge', width / 2, buttonY + buttonHeight / 2);\n        }\n    }\n\n    function formatAlertMessage(alert) {\n        if (alert.type === 'fall_alert') {\n            const person = alert.person || 'Someone';\n            return `${person} has fallen`;\n        } else if (alert.type === 'anomaly') {\n            return 'Unusual activity detected';\n        }\n        return 'Alert detected';\n    }\n\n    function calculateBounds(canvasWidth, canvasHeight) {\n        // Find bounds of all zones\n        if (currentState.zones.length === 0) {\n            // Default bounds - centered square\n            const size = Math.min(canvasWidth, canvasHeight) - config.margin * 2;\n            return {\n                x: (canvasWidth - size) / 2,\n                y: (canvasHeight - size) / 2,\n                width: size,\n                height: size,\n                scale: size / 10, // 10 meters default\n                minX: 0,\n                minY: 0\n            };\n        }\n\n        let minX = Infinity, minY = Infinity;\n        let maxX = -Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;\n\n        const d = zone.d || zone.SizeY || zone.d || 1;\n\n            minX = Math.min(minX, x);\n            minY = Math.min(minY, y);\n            maxX = Math.max(maxX, x + w);\n            maxY = Math.max(maxY, y + d);\n        });\n\n        // Add margin\n        const marginMeters = 1; // 1 meter margin\n        minX -= marginMeters;\n        minY -= marginMeters;\n        maxX += Calculate centered bounds\n        const boundsWidth = floorWidth * scale;\n        const boundsHeight = floorHeight * scale;\n        const boundsX = (canvasWidth - boundsWidth) / 2;\n        const boundsY = (canvasHeight - boundsHeight) / 2;\n\n        return {\n            x: boundsX,\n            y: boundsY,\n            width: boundsWidth,\n            height: boundsHeight,\n            scale: scale,\n            minX: minX,\n            minY: minY\n        };\n    }\n\n    function worldToScreen(wx, wy, bounds) {\n        return {\n            x: bounds.x + (wx - bounds.minX) * bounds.scale,\n            y: bounds.y + (wy - bounds.minY) * bounds.scale\n        };\n    }\n\n    function drawZones(ctx, bounds, colors) {\n        currentState.zones.forEach(zone => {\n            const x = zone.x || zone.MinX || 0;\n            const y = zone.y || zone.MinY || 0;\n            const w = zone.w || zone.SizeX || 1;\n            const d = zone.d || zone.SizeY || 1;\n\n            const topLeft = worldToScreen(x, y, bounds);\n            const width = w * bounds.scale;\n            const height = d * bounds.scale;\n\n            // Zone outline (white, 1px stroke)\n            ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffffff';\n            ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n            ctx.strokeRect(topLeft.x, topLeft.y, width, height);\n\n            // Zone label at centroid\n            const centerX = 'Zone';\n\n            ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';\n            ctx.font = '14px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';\n            ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n            ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';\n            ctx.fillText(zoneName, centerX, centerY);\n\n            if (count > 0) {\n                ctx.font = '12px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';\n                ctx.fillText(`(${count})`, centerX, centerY + 16);\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    function drawPortals(ctx, bounds, colors) {\n        if (!currentState.portals || || 0, bounds);\n\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.moveTo(p1.x, p1.y);\n            ctx.lineTo(p2.x, p2.y);\n            ctx.stroke();\n        });\n    }\n\n    function drawNodes(ctx, bounds, colors) {\n        currentState.nodes.forEach(node => {\n            const x = node.pos_x || node.PosX || 0;\n            const y = node.pos_y || node.PosY || 0;\n\n            const pos = Math.PI * 2);\n            ctx.fill();\n        });\n    }\n\n    function drawPeople(ctx, bounds, colors) {\n        currentState.blobs.forEach(blob => {\n            // Get current position (with lerp interpolation)\n            let pos = currentPositions.get(blob.id);\n            if (!pos) {\n                pos = { x: blob.x, y: blob.y, z: blob.z || 0 };\n                currentPositions.set(blob.id, pos);\n            }\n\n            // Get target position\n            const target = targetPositions.get(blob.id);\n            if (target) {\n                // Lerp target.z, LERP_FACTOR);\n\n                // Update the currentPositions map with the lerped position\n                currentPositions.set(blob.id, { ...pos });\n            }\n\n            const consistency)\n            const personName = blob.person_label || blob.person || null;\n            if (personName) {\n                blobColor = getPersonColor(personName);\n            }\n\n            // Draw person blob\n            ctx.fillStyle = blobColor;\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.arc(screenPos.x, screenPos.y, radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n            ctx.fill();\n\n            // Draw name label above\n            const name = personName ? getFirstName(personName) : '?';\n            ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';\n            ctx.font = '12px -apple-system, drawSystemStatus(ctx, colors) {\n        const size = 16; // 8px radius = 16px diameter\n        const margin = 16;\n        const x = margin + size / 2;\n        const y = margin + size / 2;\n\n health\n            const onlineNodes = currentState.nodes.filter(n => n.status === 'online').length;\n            const totalNodes = currentState.nodes.length;\n\n            if (onlineNodes === 0 && totalNodes > 0) {\n                statusColor = '#ef4444'; // Red - all offline\n            } else if (onlineNodes < totalNodes) {\n                statusColor = '#f59e0b'; // Amber - some degraded\n            } else {\n                statusColor = '#22c55e'; // Green - all healthy\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Draw status dot\n        ctx.fillStyle = statusColor;\n        ctx.beginPath();\n        ctx.arc(x, y, 8, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n        ctx.fill();\n    }\n\n    function drawTimeDisplay(ctx, canvasWidth, colors) {\n        const now = new Date();\n        const timeStr = now.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {\n            hour: 'numeric',\n            minute: '2-digit',\n            hour12: true\n        });\n\n        ctx.fillStyle = colors.text;\n        ctx.font = '28px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, monospace';\n        ctx.textAlign = 'right';\n        ctx.textBaseline = 'top';\n        ctx.fillText(timeStr, canvasWidth - 16, 16);\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Auto-Dim Logic\n    // ============================================\n\n    function resetDimTimer() {\n        if (dimTimer) {\n            clearTimeout(dimTimer);\n        }\n\n        dimTimer = setTimeout(() => {\n            enterDimMode();\n        }, AUTO_DIM_TIMEOUT_MS);\n    }\n\n    function enterDimMode() {\n        isDimmed = Entered dim mode');\n    }\n\n    function checkAmbientZonePresence() {\n        if (!config.ambientZone) {\n            return; // No ambient zone configured\n        }\n\n        // Check if anyone    // Set up event listeners\n            setupEventListeners();\n\n            // Don't check for first detection during init - it will be checked when needed\n\n  show(briefingData) {\n            if (isActive) {\n                return; // Already showing\n            }\n\n            ensureBriefingElement();\n            populateBriefing(briefingData);\n\n from API\n         */\n        async fetchAndShow() {\n            if (!(await this.shouldShowToday())) {\n                return;\n            }\n\n            try {\n                const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];\n                let briefingData;\n\n                if (onFetchBriefing) {\n                    // Use custom fetch function\n                    briefingData = await onFetchBriefing(today);\n                } else {\n                    // Default fetch from API\n                    const response = await fetch(`/api/briefing?date=${today}`);\n                    if (!response.ok) {\n                        throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);\n                    }\n                    briefingData = await response.json();\n                }\n\n                this.show(briefingData);\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error('[AmbientBriefing] Error fetching briefing:', error);\n            }\n        },\n\n        /**\n         * Set dismiss callback\n         * @param {Function} callback - Function to call when briefing is dismissed\n         */\n        setOnDismiss(callback) {\n            onDismiss = callback;\n setupEventListeners() {\n        // Dismiss button\n        const dismissBtn = document.getElementById('briefing-dismiss');\n        if (dismissBtn) {\n            // Remove any existing listeners to avoid duplicates\n            const newBtn = dismissBtn.cloneNode(true);\n            dismissBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newBtn, dismissBtn);\n\n            newBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n                AmbientBriefing.dismiss();\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Dismiss on tap/click outside content\n        if (briefingElement) {\n    }\n\n    function populateBriefing(data) {\n        const greetingEl = document.getElementById('briefing-greeting');\n        const contentEl = document.getElementById('briefing-content');\n\n    }\n\n    function parseBriefingContent(data) {\n        let html = '';\n\n        // Handle different briefing data formats\n        if (data.content) {\n            // Text content - parse for }\n                    sectionContent.push(line);\n                }\n            });\n\n            // Don't forget the last section\n            if (currentSection && sectionContent.length > 0) {\n       </div>\n        `;\n    }\n\n    function dismiss() {\n        AmbientBriefing.dismiss();\n    }\n\n    function markAsShown() {\n        const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];\n Complex CSI computation: int8 I/Q → float64 complex → amplitude/phase\n43\t  - RSSI normalization (AGC compensation): `norm = 10^((rssi_ref - rssi)/20)`\n44\t  - Spatial phase unwrapping: correct 2π jumps between adjacent subcarriers\n45\t  - Linear regression (OLS): fit `phase = a*k + b` over data subcarriers\n46\t  - STO/CFO removal: residual phase = unwrapped - (slope × k + intercept)\n47\t  - HT20 subcarrier map: 64 total, 46 data (excluding null, guard, pilot)\n48\t\n49\t- **Baseline system (`signal/baseline.go`):**\n50\t  - baseline)²))` over selected subcarriers\n62\t  - Exponential smoothing: `smooth = 0.3×raw + 0.7×prev`\n63\t  - Motion threshold: smoothDeltaRMS > 0.02\n64\t\n65\t- **Link processor (`signal/processor.go`):**\n66\t  - Complex CSI computation: int8 I/Q → float64 complex → amplitude/phase\n  - RSSI normalization (AGC compensation): `norm = 10^((rssi_ref - rssi)/20)`\n  - Spatial phase unwrapping: correct 2π jumps between adjacent subcarriers\n  - Linear regression (OLS): fit `phase = a*k + b` over data subcarriers\n  - STO/CFO removal: residual phase = unwrapped - (slope × k + intercept)\n  - HT20 subcarrier map: 64 total, 46 data (excluding null, guard, pilot)\n\n- **Baseline system (`signal/baseline.go`):**\n  - EMA baseline per link per subcarrier: `baseline = α×amplitude + (1-α)×baseline`\n  - α = dt / (τ + dt) ≈ 0.0033 for dt=0.1s, τ=30s\n  - Motion-gated updates: only update when smoothDeltaRMS < 0.05\n  - Confidence scoring: 0.3 for stale baselines (>7 days), asymptotically → 1.0\n  - Snapshot/restore for SQLite persistence\n  - BaselineManager for multi-link coordination\n\n- **Motion detection (`signal/features.go`):**\n  - NBVI (Normalized Bandwidth Variance Index): `Var(amp) / Mean(amp)²`\n  - Welford's online algorithm for numerically stable variance\n  - Top-16 subcarrier selection by NBVI score\n  - deltaRMS: `sqrt(mean((amp - baseline)²))` over selected subcarriers\n  - Exponential smoothing: `smooth = 0.3×raw + 0.7×prev`\n  - Motion threshold: smoothDeltaRMS > 0.02\n\n- **Link processor (`signal/processor.go`):**\n  - LinkProcessor: ties together phase sanitization, baseline, motion detection\n  - ProcessorManager: manages per-link processors with thread-safe access\n  - GetAllMotionStates(): returns motion state for all links\n  - GetAllBaselines()/RestoreBaseline(): for SQLite persistence\n\n**Constants used (from plan):**\n- RSSIRefdBm = -30.0\n- DefaultMotionThreshold = 0.05\n- DefaultDeltaRMSThreshold = 0.02\n- NBVITopCount = 16\n- NBVIMinThreshold = 0.001\n- DeltaRMSSmoothingAlpha = 0.3\n\n**Tests:** 37 tests covering phase sanitization, baseline, NBVI, motion detection. |\n\n### Iteration 6 — 2026-04-09\n\n**Completed:** Presence prediction for Home Assistant integration\n\nImplemented the full presence prediction system with:\n\n- **Per-person transition probability tracking (`prediction/model.go`):**\n  - `zone_transitions_history` table with all zone transitions (person_id, from_zone, to_zone, hour_of_week, dwell_duration)\n  - `transition_probabilities` table with Laplace-smoothed probabilities\n  - `dwell_times` table with mean/stddev dwell time per person/zone/hour\n  - `person_zone_entry` table for tracking current person positions\n  - Zone transition recording via `PersonZoneChange()` method\n  - Automatic probability recomputation with Laplace smoothing\n  - Dwell time statistics with mean/stddev computation\n\n- **Per-zone occupancy patterns (`prediction/accuracy.go`):**\n  - `zone_occupancy_patterns` table with occupancy_prob per zone/hour_of_week\n  - `zone_occupancy_history` table tracking entries/exits with timestamps\n  - `recorded_predictions` table for tracking prediction accuracy\n  - `accuracy_stats` table with rolling 7-day accuracy metrics\n  - Zone occupancy pattern computation from historical data\n  - Pattern-based occupancy prediction at target time\n\n- **Time-slot based predictions (`prediction/horizon.go`):**\n  - Monte Carlo simulation with 1000 runs for probabilistic predictions\n  - Multi-step path simulation accounting for dwell times\n  - Normal distribution sampling for dwell time variability\n  - Horizon predictions at 5, 15, and 30 minutes\n  - Returns probability distribution over all zones\n  - Confidence scoring based on simulation agreement\n\n- **HA sensor exposure (`mqtt/client.go`):**\n  - `PublishPredictionSensors()` creates HA auto-discovery configs\n  - `UpdatePredictionState()` publishes current predictions to MQTT\n  - Three sensors per person:\n    - `sensor.spaxel_<person>_predicted_zone` - zone name\n    - `sensor.spaxel_<person>_prediction_confidence` - percentage\n    - `sensor.spaxel_<person>_transition_minutes` - estimated minutes\n  - Topics follow HA discovery pattern: `homeassistant/sensor/.../config`\n\n- **REST API endpoints (`api/prediction.go`):**\n  - `GET /api/predictions` - Get current predictions for all people\n  - `GET /api/predictions?person=<id>&horizon=<min>` - Filtered predictions\n  - `GET /api/predictions/stats` - Transition count, data age, model readiness\n  - `POST /api/predictions/recompute` - Force probability recomputation\n  - `GET /api/predictions/accuracy` - Per-person accuracy stats\n  - `GET /api/predictions/accuracy/overall` - Overall system accuracy\n  - `GET /api/predictions/accuracy/{personID}` - Person-specific accuracy\n  - `GET /api/predictions/horizon` - Monte Carlo horizon predictions\n  - `GET /api/predictions/horizon/{personID}` - Person-specific horizon prediction\n  - `GET /api/predictions/patterns/zones` - Zone occupancy patterns\n  - `GET /api/predictions/probabilities/{personID}` - Transition probabilities\n  - `GET /api/predictions/samples/{personID}/zone/{zoneID}` - Sample counts\n\n- **Main application wiring (`cmd/mothership/main.go`):**\n  - Prediction module initialization (lines 492-534)\n  - Zone transition recording on portal crossings (lines 1579-1581)\n  - Provider wiring for zones, people, positions (lines 1831-1863)\n  - MQTT client integration for prediction publishing (lines 1846-1863)\n  - Periodic prediction update loop every 60 seconds (lines 1866-1888)\n  - Periodic prediction evaluation every 30 seconds (lines 1931-1983)\n  - REST API endpoint registration (lines 2527-2888)\n\n**Constants and thresholds:**\n- MinimumDataAge = 7 days (168 hours) before predictions activate\n- MinimumSamplesPerSlot = 3 observations per time slot\n- PredictionHorizon = 15 minutes (default)\n- MonteCarloRuns = 1000 simulations\n- TargetAccuracy = 75% at 15-minute horizon\n\n**Accuracy tracking:**\n- Records predictions when made (personID, currentZone, predictedZone, confidence, horizon)\n- Evaluates pending predictions when target time is reached\n- Compares predicted zone vs actual zone\n- Computes rolling 7-day accuracy percentage\n- Reports \"meets_target\" when accuracy ≥ 75% and min predictions threshold met\n\n**Model learning:**\n- Observations recorded every 5 minutes per person/zone\n- EMA update: `p_new = p_old + α × (obs - p_old)` where α = 0.03\n- Cold start: 7 days of data required for model readiness\n- Slot ready when sample_count ≥ 3\n- Automatic recomputation triggered on zone transitions\n\n**Files propagation model with path loss + wall penetration + first-order reflections\n- GDOP computation per cell using Fisher information matrix\n- REST API at `/api/simulator/*` for space/node/walker management and GDOP computation\n\n**CSI simulator CLI (`cmd/sim/`):**\n- Connects to mothership as virtual nodes, sends synthetic CSI binary frames\n- Walker random-walk model with Gaussian velocity updates, wall reflection\n- Amplitude/phase generated from propagation model with Gaussian noise injection\n- Optional BLE advertisement simulation (`--ble` flag)\n- Verified authentication (exits non-zero on `{type:\"reject\"}`)\n- Integration test support: polls `GET /api/blobs` for blob count assertions\n\n**Fresnel zone debug overlay (`dashboard/js/fresnel.js`):**\n- Toggle-able wireframe ellipsoids between active TX/RX link pairs\n- Ellipsoid geometry computed from TX/RX positions and Fresnel zone number\n- Color-coded by zone number (zone 1 = bright, outer zones = dimmer)\n- Toolbar button integration with existing layers panel\n\n**Files created/modified:**\n```\nmothership/internal/timeline/       — timeline.go, timeline_test.go, handler.go, expert mode only\n\n**Morning briefing (`internal/briefing/`, `dashboard/js/briefing.js`):**\n- `Generator` assembles briefing in priority order from sleep, events, anomalies, system health\n- Priority blocks: critical alerts → sleep summary → who is home → overnight anomalies → system health → predictions → learning progress\n- Degenerate case: \"All quiet last night. connectivity → show link health → suggest repositioning → offer re-baseline\n- First-time feature tooltips shown once, dismissed on click, stored in `localStorage`\n- Post-feedback explanations in
